                    </div>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="book-info-about-audience float-right">\n                    \n    <div class="book-info-bottom-indetail book-page-content float-right">\n        <h2>Video Description</h2>\n        <div class="book-info-bottom-indetail-text" itemprop="description">\n            <p><span id="description" class="sugar_field">Routing is a very important component of the web or native applications as it affects the power and usability of the application. Most web applications need to support different URLs to navigate users to different pages in the application. Thats where a router comes in.</span></p>\n<p><span id="description" class="sugar_field">This course is a simple way to get started with Angular Router and harness its full power for your applications. Its a JavaScript router implementation thats designed to work with Angular and is packaged as @angular/router. By using Angular Router, you will activate all required Angular components to compose a page when a user navigates to a certain URL. </span></p>\n<p><span id="description" class="sugar_field">Youll learn to set up routing so that it lets users navigate from one page to another without page reload. Instead, it updates the browsers history so the user can use the back and forward buttons when navigating between pages. In addition, youll do tasks such as redirect a URL to another URL, resolve data before a page is displayed, run scripts when a page is activated or deactivated, and lazy load the parts of our application.</span></p>\n<p><span id="description" class="sugar_field">By the end of this course, youll be ready to work on projects with Angular Router and make routing configuration work in your Angular application.<br /></span></p>\n<p><span id="description" class="sugar_field">The code bundle for this video course is available at- <a href="https://github.com/PacktPublishing/Hands-On-Angular-Routing" target="_new">https://github.com/PacktPublishing/Hands-On-Angular-Routing</a></span></p>\n<h1><span class="sugar_field">Style and Approach</span></h1>\n<p><span class="sugar_field"><span id="trade_selling_points_c" class="sugar_field">The course takes a hands-on approach, creating an interesting and illustrative application to demonstrate the concepts, while only necessary jargon and theory will be discussed.</span></span></p>\n\n        </div>\n    </div>\n                    \n    <div class="book-info-bottom-indetail class="book-info-bottom-wrapper section-inner cf">\n\t\t\t\t<div id="book-info-will-learn" class="float-right book-page-content">\n\t\t\t\t\t<h2>What You Will Learn</h2>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class="book-info-will-learn-text">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<ul>\n<li>Explore the foundations of Angular Routing using practical real-world applications</li>\n<li>Get the route parameter from your current route and the external route by learning more about routing parameters</li>\n<li>Fetch data before navigating to the route using Route Resolver</li>\n<li>Implement child routes in Angular Application by understanding how some routes may only be accessible and viewed within other routes</li>\n<li>Style, animate and watch the routes</li>\n<li>Protecting your routes using Route Guards</li>\n<li>Improve the performance of your Angular application using lazy loading</li>\n</ul>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\t\t\t\t<div class="book-info-bottom-author book-page-content href="https://subscription.packtpub.com/video/web_development/9781838646868/103756/103775/animating-routes-in-action" target="_blank">\n                                                    <div class="book-toc-section cf">\n                                                        <div class="book-toc-section-circle float-left"></div>\n                                                        <div class="book-toc-section-text float-left">Animating Routes in Action</div>\n                                                    </div>\n                                                </a>\n                                                                                    </div>\n                                    </div>\n                                                            </div>\n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="book-info-about-audience float-right">\n                    \n    <div class="book-info-bottom-indetail book-page-content float-right">\n        <h2>Video Description</h2>\n        <div class="book-info-bottom-indetail-text" itemprop="description">\n            <p><span id="description" class="sugar_field">Routing is a very important component of the web or native applications as it affects the power and usability of the application. Most web applications need to support different URLs to navigate users to different pages in the application. Thats where a router comes in.</span></p>\n<p><span id="description" class="sugar_field">This course is a simple way to get started with Angular Router and harness its full power for your applications. Its a JavaScript router implementation thats designed to work with Angular and is packaged as @angular/router. By using Angular Router, you will activate all required Angular components to compose a page when a user navigates to a certain URL. </span></p>\n<p><span id="description" class="sugar_field">Youll learn to set up routing so that it lets users navigate from one page to another without page reload. Instead, it updates the browsers history so the user can use the back and forward buttons when navigating between pages. In addition, youll do tasks such as redirect a URL to another URL, resolve data before a page is displayed, run scripts when a page is activated or deactivated, and lazy load the parts of our application.</span></p>\n<p><span id="description" class="sugar_field">By the end of this course, youll be ready to work on projects with Angular Router and make routing configuration work in your Angular application.<br /></span></p>\n<p><span id="description" class="sugar_field">The code bundle for this video course is available at- <a href="https://github.com/PacktPublishing/Hands-On-Angular-Routing" target="_new">https://github.com/PacktPublishing/Hands-On-Angular-Routing</a></span></p>\n<h1><span class="sugar_field">Style and Approach</span></h1>\n<p><span class="sugar_field"><span id="trade_selling_points_c" class="sugar_field">The course takes a hands-on approach, creating an interesting and illustrative application to demonstrate the concepts, while only necessary jargon and theory will be discussed.</span></span></p>\n\n        </div>\n    </div>\n                    \n    <div class="book-info-bottom-indetail book-page-content float-right">\n        <h2 id="video-preview-header">Video Preview</h2>\n        <p>\n            <video src="https://d1ft11egbn8l.cloudfront.net/Hands On Angular class="book-info-bottom-wrapper section-inner cf">\n\t\t\t\t<div id="book-info-will-learn" class="float-right book-page-content">\n\t\t\t\t\t<h2>What You Will Learn</h2>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class="book-info-will-learn-text">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<ul>\n<li>Explore the foundations of Angular Routing using practical real-world applications</li>\n<li>Get the route parameter from your current route and the external route by learning more about routing parameters</li>\n<li>Fetch data before navigating to the route using Route Resolver</li>\n<li>Implement child routes in Angular Application by understanding how some routes may only be accessible and viewed within other routes</li>\n<li>Style, animate and watch the routes</li>\n<li>Protecting your routes using Route Guards</li>\n<li>Improve the performance of your Angular application using lazy loading</li>\n</ul>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\t\t\t\t<div class="book-info-bottom-author book-page-content
